# 📐 Square-1 Cubeshape Parity (CSP) Algorithms Reference Sheet

This sheet lists all the **SQ1 CSP** cases sorted by subsets (Slashes). Each case includes the **top and bottom layer diagrams** corresponding to the shape, generated dynamically.
